        $('.content-find').click(function () {
            $('.content-container').html('');
            page = 1; 
            sort = "None"; 
            loadContent();
        });

        function loadContent() {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/load-content',
                type: "POST",
                data: {
                    Search: $('#content-name').val(),
                    Type: $('#content-type').val(),
                    PageNumber: page,
                    SortState: sort
                },
                success: function (result) {
                    $('.content-container').append(result);
                }
            });
        }

        function sorting(me) {
            $('.content-container').html('');
            page = 1; 
            sort = $(me).data("sort");
            loadContent();
        }

        function addContent(me) {
            page += 1;
            loadContent();
        }
    </script>

                slidesToScroll: 1,

        $('.content-find').click(function () {
            $('.content-container').html('');
            page = 1; 
            sort = "None"; 
            loadContent();
        });

        function loadContent() {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/load-content',
                type: "POST",
                data: {
                    Search: $('#content-name').val(),
                    Type: $('#content-type').val(),
                    PageNumber: page,
                    SortState: sort
                },
                success: function (result) {
                    $('.content-container').append(result);
                }
            });
        }

        function sorting(me) {
            $('.content-container').html('');
            page = 1; 
            sort = $(me).data("sort");
            loadContent();
        }

        function addContent(me) {
            page += 1;
            loadContent();
        }
    </script>
